## `alpha_bar`

**Author kwarg:** `alpha_bar` (passed on `DearPyGuiUiLibrary.C.*` emitters or `mount(...)`).

**Used by:** [`DpgColorEdit`](entities.md#entity-dpgcoloredit), [`DpgColorPicker`](entities.md#entity-dpgcolorpicker)

| Emitter (kind) | Author kwarg | Native setter / binding | Mode | Setter kind | Notes |
|------------------|--------------|-------------------------|------|-------------|-------|
| `DpgColorEdit` | `alpha_bar` | `DearPyGui` factory / item ctor `alpha_bar=...` | `constructor` | `ctor` | annotation `bool` |
| `DpgColorEdit` | `alpha_bar` | `dpg.configure(item, alpha_bar=...)` | `PropMode.CREATE_UPDATE` | `AccessorKind.DPG_CONFIG` | setter API `alpha_bar`; ctor field `alpha_bar` |
| `DpgColorPicker` | `alpha_bar` | `DearPyGui` factory / item ctor `alpha_bar=...` | `constructor` | `ctor` | annotation `bool` |
| `DpgColorPicker` | `alpha_bar` | `dpg.configure(item, alpha_bar=...)` | `PropMode.CREATE_UPDATE` | `AccessorKind.DPG_CONFIG` | setter API `alpha_bar`; ctor field `alpha_bar` |

<a id="prop-enabled"></a>
